                  <div jsname="bVEB4e" class="wWOJcd" aria-controls="exacc_m6jmY7XvJLWy2roPkK2R8AQ_4" aria-expanded="false" aria-labelledby="exacc_m6jmY7XvJLWy2roPkK2R8AQ_3" role="button" tabindex="0" jsaction="AWEk5c">

                    <span>Why is the NZ flag red on boats?</span>

                   </div>

                   <div jsname="Q8Kwad" class="YsGUOb"></div>

                   <div jsname="K8Pnod" class="r21Kzd" data-hveid="CCYQAQ" data-ved="2ahUKEwj1qIGS5Yv9AhU1mVYBHZBWBE4Quk56BAgmEAE"></div>

                   <div jsname="Fus96e" class="guvigf" data-ved="2ahUKEwj1qIGS5Yv9AhU1mVYBHZBWBE4Q36YDegQIJhAC"></div>

                  </div>

                  <div jsname="rozPHf" class="MBtdbb" id="exacc_m6jmY7XvJLWy2roPkK2R8AQ_4" data-ved="2ahUKEwj1qIGS5Yv9AhU1mVYBHZBWBE4Q7NUEegQIJhAD">

                   <div class="ymu2Hb" jsslot="">

                    <div jsname="oQYOj" class="t0bRye r2fjmd" id="_m6jmY7XvJLWy2roPkK2R8AQ_35" data-hveid="CCYQBA" data-ved="2ahUKEwj1qIGS5Yv9AhU1mVYBHZBWBE4Qu04oAHoECCYQBA">

                     <div id="m6jmY7XvJLWy2roPkK2R8AQ__40">

                      <div class="wDYxhc" data-md="61" style="clear:none">

                       <div class="LGOjhe" data-attrid="wa:/description" aria-level="3" role="heading" data-hveid="CCIQAA">

                        <span class="ILfuVd" lang="en"><span class="hgKElc">The New Zealand Red Ensign, adopted in 1903, is <b>based on the Red Ensign (colloquially known as the 'red duster') that has been flown for centuries by merchant ships registered in the United Kingdom</b>. Merchant ships registered in New Zealand initially carried the Red Ensign.</span></span>
